605| // ========== SECTION SIGNALEMENTS ==========
606| async function loadReports() {
607|     const reportsDiv = document.getElementById('reportsList');
608|     if (!reportsDiv) return;
609| 
610|     try {
611|         const response = await fetch('/api/admin/reports');
612|         const reports = await response.json();
613| 
614|         if (reports.length === 0) {
615|             reportsDiv.innerHTML = '<div class="loading">✅ Aucun signalement en attente</div>';
616|             return;
617|         }
618| 
619|         let html = '<table class="admin-table"><thead><tr><th>Date</th><th>Signalé par</th><th>Cible</th><th>Actions</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
620| 
621|         reports.forEach(r => {
622|             html += `
623|                 <tr>
624|                     <td>${new Date(r.created_at).toLocaleString()}</td>
625|                     <td>${escapeHtml(r.reporter_pseudo)}</td>
626|                     <td><strong>${escapeHtml(r.target_pseudo)}</strong></td>
627|                     <td class="action-buttons">
628|                         <button class="action-btn btn-warn" onclick="warnUser('${escapeHtml(r.target_pseudo)}')">⚠️ Warn</button>
629|                         <button class="action-btn btn-ban" onclick="banUser('${escapeHtml(r.target_pseudo)}')">🚫 Ban</button>
630|                         <button class="action-btn btn-ignore" onclick="ignoreReport(${r.id})">✅ Ignorer</button>
631|                     </td>
632|                 </tr>
633|             `;
634|         });
635| 
636|         html += '</tbody></table>';
637|         reportsDiv.innerHTML = html;
638|     } catch (err) {
639|         console.error(err);
640|         reportsDiv.innerHTML = '<div class="loading">❌ Erreur chargement</div>';
641|     }
642| }
643| 
644| async function ignoreReport(reportId) {
645|     if (typeof MGModal !== 'undefined') {
646|         MGModal.show({
647|             title: '✅ Ignorer',
648|             message: 'Ignorer ce signalement ?',
649|             onConfirm: async () => {
650|                 try {
651|                     const response = await fetch('/api/admin/ignore-report', {
652|                         method: 'POST',
653|                         headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
654|                         body: JSON.stringify({ reportId })
655|                     });
656| 
657|                     if (response.ok) {
658|                         MGModal.show({
659|                             title: '✅ Ignoré',
660|                             message: 'Signalement ignoré.',
661|                             onConfirm: () => loadReports()
662|                         });
663|                     } else {
664|                         MGModal.show({
665|                             title: '❌ Erreur',
666|                             message: 'Erreur lors de l\'ignorance.',
667|                             onConfirm: () => { }
668|                         });
669|                     }
670|                 } catch (err) {
671|                     console.error(err);
672|                     MGModal.show({
673|                         title: '❌ Erreur réseau',
674|                         message: 'Impossible de contacter le serveur.',
675|                         onConfirm: () => { }
676|                     });
677|                 }
678|             },
679|             onCancel: () => { }
680|         });
681|     } else {
682|         // Fallback
683|         if (!confirm('Ignorer ce signalement ?')) return;
684|         try {
685|             const response = await fetch('/api/admin/ignore-report', {
686|                 method: 'POST',
687|                 headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
688|                 body: JSON.stringify({ reportId })
689|             });
690|             if (response.ok) {
691|                 alert('✅ Signalement ignoré');
692|                 loadReports();
693|             } else {
694|                 alert('❌ Erreur');
695|             }
696|         } catch (err) {
697|             console.error(err);
698|             alert('❌ Erreur réseau');
699|         }
700|     }
701| }
702| 
703| // ========== SECTION JOURNAL ==========
704| async function loadModerationLogs() {
705|     const logsDiv = document.getElementById('logsList');
706|     if (!logsDiv) return;
707| 
708|     try {
709|         const response = await fetch('/api/admin/moderation-logs');
710|         const logs = await response.json();
711| 
712|         if (logs.length === 0) {
713|             logsDiv.innerHTML = '<div class="loading">📭 Aucune action enregistrée</div>';
714|             return;
715|         }
716| 
717|         let html = '<table class="admin-table"><thead><tr><th>Date</th><th>Admin</th><th>Action</th><th>Cible</th><th>Détails</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
718| 
719|         logs.forEach(log => {
720|             let actionIcon = '';
721|             if (log.action_type === 'warn') actionIcon = '⚠️';
722|             else if (log.action_type === 'ban') actionIcon = '🚫';
723|             else if (log.action_type === 'temp_ban') actionIcon = '⏱️';
724|             else if (log.action_type === 'unban') actionIcon = '🔓';
725|             else if (log.action_type === 'set_modo') actionIcon = '👮';
726|             else if (log.action_type === 'set_admin') actionIcon = '👑';
727|             else actionIcon = '📝';
728| 
729|             let details = log.reason || '';
730|             if (log.duration_minutes) details += ` (${log.duration_minutes} min)`;
731| 
732|             html += `
733|                 <tr>
734|                     <td>${new Date(log.created_at).toLocaleString()}</td>
735|                     <td>${escapeHtml(log.admin_pseudo)}</td>
736|                     <td>${actionIcon} ${escapeHtml(log.action_type)}</td>
737|                     <td><strong>${escapeHtml(log.target_pseudo)}</strong></td>
738|                     <td>${escapeHtml(details)}</td>
739|                 </tr>
740|             `;
741|         });
742| 
743|         html += '</tbody></table>';
744|         logsDiv.innerHTML = html;
745|     } catch (err) {
746|         console.error(err);
747|         logsDiv.innerHTML = '<div class="loading">❌ Erreur chargement</div>';
748|     }
749| 
750| }

879| // ========== HORLOGE EN TEMPS RÉEL ==========
880| function updateClock() {
881|     const now = new Date();
882|     const options = {
883|         weekday: 'long',
884|         year: 'numeric',
885|         month: 'long',
886|         day: 'numeric',
887|         hour: '2-digit',
888|         minute: '2-digit',
889|         second: '2-digit',
890|         hour12: false
891|     };
892|     const formatted = now.toLocaleDateString('fr-FR', options);
893|     const clockSpan = document.getElementById('currentDateTime');
894|     if (clockSpan) clockSpan.textContent = formatted;
895| }
896| 
897| // Mettre à jour l'horloge toutes les secondes
898| setInterval(updateClock, 1000);
899| updateClock(); // Appel immédiat
900| 
901| // Gestion des onglets
902| function initTabs() {
903|     const tabs = document.querySelectorAll('.tab-btn');
904|     tabs.forEach(btn => {
905|         btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
906|             tabs.forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
907|             btn.classList.add('active');
908| 
909|             document.querySelectorAll('.tab-content').forEach(content => {
910|                 content.classList.remove('active');
911|             });
912| 
913|             const tabId = `tab-${btn.dataset.tab}`;
914|             document.getElementById(tabId).classList.add('active');
915| 
916|             if (btn.dataset.tab === 'reports') loadReports();
917|             if (btn.dataset.tab === 'logs') loadModerationLogs();
918|         });
919|     });
920| }

922| // ========== 7. UTILITAIRES ==========
923| function escapeHtml(str) {
924|     if (!str) return '';
925|     return str.replace(/[&<>]/g, function (m) {
926|         if (m === '&') return '&amp;';
927|         if (m === '<') return '&lt;';
928|         if (m === '>') return '&gt;';
929|         return m;
930|     });
931| }

3| let currentReceivedMessage = null;
4| let currentReceivedFrom = null;
5| 
6| function displayMessage(text, type, fromPseudo = null, targetName = null) {
7|     const messageArea = document.getElementById('messageArea');
8|     if (!messageArea) return;
9| 
10|     messageArea.innerHTML = '';
11|     const div = document.createElement('div');
12|     div.className = 'current-message';
13| 
14|     if (type === 'received') {
15|         div.innerHTML = `<strong>✉️ ${escapeHtml(fromPseudo)} :</strong> ${escapeHtml(text)}`;
16|         div.style.background = '#fff0e0';
17|         div.style.padding = '15px';
18|         div.style.borderRadius = '12px';
19|         currentReceivedMessage = text;
20|         currentReceivedFrom = fromPseudo;
21|     } else if (type === 'sent') {
22|         div.innerHTML = `<strong>📤 Vous → ${escapeHtml(targetName)} :</strong> ${escapeHtml(text)}`;
23|         div.style.background = '#e0f0ff';
24|         div.style.padding = '15px';
25|         div.style.borderRadius = '12px';
26|         currentReceivedMessage = null;
27|         currentReceivedFrom = null;
28|     }
29| 
30|     messageArea.appendChild(div);
31| }
32| 
33| function clearMessageArea() {
34|     const messageArea = document.getElementById('messageArea');
35|     const t = window.chatT || { emptyMessage: "💬 En attente de message..." };
36|     if (messageArea) {
37|         messageArea.innerHTML = `<div class="empty-message">${t.emptyMessage}</div>`;
38|     }
39|     currentReceivedMessage = null;
40|     currentReceivedFrom = null;
41| }

43| function showContactInfo(pseudo, age, origine, gender, orientation, location, purpose, bio) {
44|     const contactInfoDiv = document.getElementById('contactInfo');
45|     const contactNameSpan = document.getElementById('contactName');
46|     const contactAgeSpan = document.getElementById('contactAge');
47|     const contactGenderSpan = document.getElementById('contactGender');
48|     const contactOrientationSpan = document.getElementById('contactOrientation');
49|     const contactPurposeDiv = document.getElementById('contactPurpose');
50|     const contactBioSpan = document.getElementById('contactBio');
51| 
52|     if (!contactInfoDiv) return;
53| 
54|     contactInfoDiv.style.display = 'block';
55| 
56|     // 1. Pseudo
57|     if (contactNameSpan) contactNameSpan.innerText = pseudo || '?';
58| 
59|     // 2. Âge
60|     if (contactAgeSpan) {
61|         const origineText = (origine && origine !== 'undefined' && origine !== '' && origine !== null) ? `<i class="fas fa-globe"></i> ${origine}` : '';
62|         contactAgeSpan.innerHTML = `<i class="fas fa-birthday-cake"></i> ${age || '?'} ans, ${origineText}`;
63|     }
64| 
65|     // 3. Genre
66|     let genderText = '?';
67|     if (gender === 'G') genderText = 'Gay';
68|     else if (gender === 'H') genderText = (window.chatLang === 'fr' ? 'Hétéro' : 'Hetero');
69|     else if (gender === 'T') genderText = (window.chatLang === 'fr' ? 'Transgenre' : 'Transgender');
70|     if (contactGenderSpan) contactGenderSpan.innerText = genderText;
71| 
72|     // 4. Orientation
73|     const orientationText = getOrientationText(orientation) || '?';
74|     if (contactOrientationSpan) contactOrientationSpan.innerText = orientationText;
75| 
76|     // 5. Localité (on l'ajoute à la suite de l'orientation)
77|     const locationText = (location && location !== 'undefined') ? location : '';
78|     if (locationText && contactOrientationSpan) {
79|         // On ajoute la localité après l'orientation
80|         contactOrientationSpan.innerText = `${orientationText} | ${locationText}`;
81|     }
82| 
83|     // 6. Objectif
84|     let purposeText = '';
85|     if (purpose === 'meeting') purposeText = (window.chatLang === 'fr' ? '💬 Rencontre' : '💬 Ontmoeting');
86|     else if (purpose === 'flirt') purposeText = (window.chatLang === 'fr' ? '😘 Flirt' : '😘 Flirt');
87|     else if (purpose === 'adultery') purposeText = (window.chatLang === 'fr' ? '💔 Relation sexuelle' : '💔 Seksuele relatie');
88|     else purposeText = (window.chatLang === 'fr' ? 'Non précisé' : 'Niet gespecificeerd');
89| 
90|     if (contactPurposeDiv) {
91|         contactPurposeDiv.innerHTML = `🎯 Je suis ici pour : ${purposeText}`;
92|     }
93| 
94|     // 7. Bio
95|     if (contactBioSpan) {
96|         contactBioSpan.innerText = bio || (window.chatLang === 'fr' ? 'Pas de présentation' : 'Geen introductie');
97|     }            // Supprimer l'ancienne icône si elle existe
98|     const oldIcon = document.querySelector('[id^="reportIcon_"]');
99|     if (oldIcon) oldIcon.remove();
100| 
101|     // Ajouter la nouvelle icône
102|     const firstDiv = document.querySelector('#contactInfo div:first-child');
103|     if (firstDiv && !document.getElementById('reportIcon_' + pseudo)) {
104|         const icon = document.createElement('span');
105|         icon.id = 'reportIcon_' + pseudo;
106|         icon.textContent = ' ⚠️';
107|         icon.style.cursor = 'pointer';
108|         icon.style.opacity = '0.6';
109|         icon.style.marginLeft = '4px';
110|         icon.style.fontSize = '0.9rem';
111|         icon.title = `Signaler ${pseudo}`;
112|         icon.onclick = (e) => {
113|             e.stopPropagation();
114|             if (typeof socket !== 'undefined' && pseudo) {
115|                 if (typeof MGModal !== 'undefined') {
116|                     MGModal.show({
117|                         title: '⚠️ Confirmation de signalement',
118|                         message: `Voulez-vous vraiment signaler ${pseudo} ?\n\nUn modérateur examinera ce signalement.\n\nCette action est irréversible.`,
119|                         onConfirm: () => {
120|                             socket.emit('report user', { targetPseudo: pseudo });
121|                             MGModal.show({
122|                                 title: '✅ Signalement envoyé',
123|                                 message: `Merci d'avoir signalé ${pseudo}.\n\nL'équipe de modération va examiner.`,
124|                                 onConfirm: () => { }
125|                             });
126|                         },
127|                         onCancel: () => {
128|                             MGModal.show({
129|                                 title: '❌ Annulé',
130|                                 message: `Signalement de ${pseudo} annulé.`,
131|                                 onConfirm: () => { }
132|                             });
133|                         }
134|                     });
135|                 } else {
136|                     // Fallback si MGModal n'existe pas
137|                     if (confirm(`⚠️ Signaler ${pseudo} ?`)) {
138|                         socket.emit('report user', { targetPseudo: pseudo });
139|                         alert(`✅ Signalement envoyé pour ${pseudo}`);
140|                     }
141|                 }
142|             } else {
143|                 alert('❌ Impossible de signaler pour le moment');
144|             }
145|         };
146|         firstDiv.appendChild(icon);
147|     }
148| }

156| function updateEnvelope(pendingCount) {
157|     const envelope = document.getElementById('envelope');
158|     if (!envelope) return;
159| 
160|     if (pendingCount > 0) {
161|         envelope.style.display = 'flex';
162|         const oldBadge = envelope.querySelector('.pending-badge');
163|         if (oldBadge) oldBadge.remove();
164|         const badge = document.createElement('span');
165|         badge.className = 'pending-badge';
166|         badge.textContent = pendingCount;
167|         envelope.appendChild(badge);
168|     } else {
169|         envelope.style.display = 'none';
170|     }
171| }

25|     function setupButtons(onConfirm, onCancel) {
26|         const confirmBtn = document.getElementById('mg-modal-confirm');
27|         const cancelBtn = document.getElementById('mg-modal-cancel');
28|         const container = document.getElementById('mg-modal-container');
29| 
30|         if (confirmBtn) {
31|             const newConfirm = confirmBtn.cloneNode(true);
32|             confirmBtn.parentNode.replaceChild(newConfirm, confirmBtn);
33|             newConfirm.onclick = () => {
34|                 container.style.display = 'none';
35|                 if (onConfirm) onConfirm();
36|             };
37|         }
38| 
39|         if (cancelBtn) {
40|             const newCancel = cancelBtn.cloneNode(true);
41|             cancelBtn.parentNode.replaceChild(newCancel, cancelBtn);
42|             newCancel.onclick = () => {
43|                 container.style.display = 'none';
44|                 if (onCancel) onCancel();
45|             };
46|         }
47| 
48|         container.onclick = (e) => {
49|             if (e.target === container) {
50|                 container.style.display = 'none';
51|                 if (onCancel) onCancel();
52|             }
53|         };
54|     }
55| 
56|     window.MGModal = {
57|         show: function (options) {
58|             createModalStructure();
59| 
60|             const container = document.getElementById('mg-modal-container');
61|             const box = document.getElementById('mg-modal-box');
62|             const titleEl = document.getElementById('mg-modal-title');
63|             const messageEl = document.getElementById('mg-modal-message');
64| 
65|             titleEl.textContent = options.title || '⚠️ Attention';
66|             messageEl.textContent = options.message || 'Message par défaut';
67| 
68|             setupButtons(options.onConfirm, options.onCancel);
69| 
70|             container.style.display = 'flex';
71| 
72|             setTimeout(() => {
73|                 if (box) {
74|                     box.style.transform = 'translateY(0)';
75|                     box.style.opacity = '1';
76|                 }
77|             }, 10);
78|         },
79| 
80|         hide: function () {
81|             const container = document.getElementById('mg-modal-container');
82|             if (container) container.style.display = 'none';
83|         }
84|     };
85| })();

100| // ========== RÉCUPÉRATION DES INFOS UTILISATEUR DEPUIS LA BASE ==========00000

104| async function initUser() {
105|     console.log('1. Début initUser');
106|     if (!storedUser || !storedUser.pseudo) {
107|         console.log('2. Pas de storedUser');
108|         window.location.href = '/login.html';
109|         return;
110|     }
111| 
112|     try {
113|         console.log('3. Appel fetch pour pseudo:', storedUser.pseudo);
114|         const response = await fetch('/api/get-user', {
115|             method: 'POST',
116|             headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
117|             body: JSON.stringify({ pseudo: storedUser.pseudo })
118|         });
119|         console.log('4. Réponse reçue, status:', response.status);
120|         const data = await response.json();
121|         console.log('5. Data reçue:', data);
122|         if (data.success) {
123|             user = data.user;
124|             localStorage.setItem('meetgay_user_full', JSON.stringify(user));
125|             console.log('6. Utilisateur chargé, démarrage chat');
126|             startChat();
127|         } else {
128|             console.log('7. Pas de success');
129|             window.location.href = '/login.html';
130|         }
131|     } catch (err) {
132|         console.error('Erreur:', err);
133|         window.location.href = '/login.html';
134|     }
135| }

137| // ========== DÉMARRAGE DU CHAT (après récupération des infos) ==========
138| function startChat() {
139|     if (typeof conversationHistory === 'undefined') {
140|         window.conversationHistory = {};
141|     }
142| 
143|     if ('serviceWorker' in navigator) {
144|         navigator.serviceWorker.register('/sw.js').then(reg => {
145|             console.log('SW enregistré');
146|             if (reg.active) {
147|                 reg.active.postMessage({ action: 'userConnected', connected: true });
148|             } else {
149|                 reg.installing?.postMessage({ action: 'userConnected', connected: true });
150|             }
151|         });
152|     }
153|     // Charger l'historique des messages pour une conversation
154|     async function loadHistory(withPseudo) {
155|         try {
156|             const response = await fetch(`/api/messages/${encodeURIComponent(user.pseudo)}/${encodeURIComponent(withPseudo)}`);
157|             const messages = await response.json();
158| 
159|             // Nettoyer l'historique existant pour ce contact
160|             if (!conversationHistory[withPseudo]) {
161|                 conversationHistory[withPseudo] = [];
162|             } else {
163|                 conversationHistory[withPseudo] = [];
164|             }
165| 
166|             // Ajouter les messages chargés
167|             messages.forEach(msg => {
168|                 const type = msg.from_pseudo === user.pseudo ? 'sent' : 'received';
169|                 conversationHistory[withPseudo].push({
170|                     text: msg.message,
171|                     type: type,
172|                     from: msg.from_pseudo,
173|                     to: msg.to_pseudo,
174|                     timestamp: new Date(msg.created_at)
175|                 });
176|             });
177| 
178|             updateHistoryDisplay();
179|         } catch (err) {
180|             console.error('Erreur chargement historique:', err);
181|         }
182| 
183|     }
184|

186|     const messageInput = document.getElementById('messageInput');
187|     const sendBtn = document.getElementById('sendBtn');
188|     const envelope = document.getElementById('envelope');
189| 
190|     // Bouton déconnexion
191|     const logoutBtn = document.getElementById('logoutBtn');
192|     if (logoutBtn) {
193|         logoutBtn.onclick = async () => {
194|             try {
195|                 await fetch('/api/delete-user', {
196|                     method: 'POST',
197|                     headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
198|                     body: JSON.stringify({ pseudo: user.pseudo })
199|                 });
200|             } catch (err) {
201|                 console.error('Erreur suppression utilisateur:', err);
202|             }
203| 
204|             localStorage.removeItem('meetgay_token');
205|             localStorage.removeItem('meetgay_user');
206|             localStorage.removeItem('meetgay_user_full');
207|             socket.disconnect();
208| 
209|             // Envoie le message AVANT de quitter la page
210|             navigator.serviceWorker.ready.then(reg => {
211|                 if (reg.active) {
212|                     reg.active.postMessage({ action: 'userConnected', connected: false });
213|                 }
214|                 // Une fois le message envoyé, on redirige
215|                 window.location.href = '/login.html';
216|             });
217|         };  // ← cette accolade ferme logoutBtn.onclick = ...
218|     }  // ← cette accolade ferme if (logoutBtn)

229|         const userBadge = document.getElementById('userBadge');
230|         if (!userBadge) return;

232|         // Récupérer la ville
233|         const city = user.location_name || user.location_code || '?';
234| 
235|         // Afficher le triangle seulement si warnsCount > 0
236|         if (warnsCount > 0) {
237|             const triangleColor = getTriangleColor(warnsCount);
238|             userBadge.innerHTML = `👤 ${escapeHtml(user.pseudo)} | ${escapeHtml(city)} <span style="color: ${triangleColor}; margin-left: 8px;">⚠️ ${warnsCount}</span>`;
239|         } else {

241|         }
242|     }

244|     function getTriangleColor(warns) {
245|         if (warns >= 3) return '#ff0000';      // rouge
246|         if (warns === 2) return '#ff6600';     // orange foncé
247|         if (warns === 1) return '#ffaa00';     // orange clair
248|         return '#888888';                       // gris
249|     }

509|     function showPrivatePopup(pseudo) {
510|         if (document.getElementById('privatePopup')) return;
511| 
512|         const chatPanel = document.querySelector('.chat-panel');
513|         if (!chatPanel) return;
514| 
515|         if (getComputedStyle(chatPanel).position !== 'relative') {
516|             chatPanel.style.position = 'relative';
517|         }
518| 
519|         const inputArea = document.querySelector('.input-area');
520|         if (!inputArea) return;
521| 
522|         const inputRect = inputArea.getBoundingClientRect();
523|         const chatRect = chatPanel.getBoundingClientRect();
524|         const topPosition = inputRect.bottom - chatRect.top;
525| 
526|         const popup = document.createElement('div');
527|         popup.id = 'privatePopup';
528|         popup.style.cssText = `
529|             position: absolute;
530|             top: ${topPosition + 5}px;
531|             left: 0;
532|             right: 0;
533|             background: #2c3e50;
534|             color: white;
535|             border-radius: 8px;
536|             padding: 10px 12px;
537|             z-index: 1000;
538|             font-family: 'Segoe UI', sans-serif;
539|             font-size: 12px;
540|             display: flex;
541|             justify-content: space-between;
542|             align-items: center;
543|             flex-wrap: wrap;
544|             gap: 8px;
545|             box-shadow: 0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.15);
546|             opacity: 0;
547|             transform: translateY(-10px);
548|             transition: opacity 0.2s ease, transform 0.2s ease;
549|         `;
550| 
551|         popup.innerHTML = `
552|             <span>💬 <strong>${pseudo}</strong> : 3 messages échangés. Passer en privé ?</span>
553|             <div style="display: flex; gap: 6px;">
554|                 <button id="popupAccept" style="background:#27ae60; color:white; border:none; border-radius:4px; padding:4px 10px; cursor:pointer;">✅ Oui</button>
555|                 <button id="popupDecline" style="background:#e74c3c; color:white; border:none; border-radius:4px; padding:4px 10px; cursor:pointer;">❌ Non</button>
556|             </div>
557|         `;
558| 
559|         chatPanel.appendChild(popup);
560| 
561|         setTimeout(() => {
562|             popup.style.opacity = '1';
563|             popup.style.transform = 'translateY(0)';
564|         }, 10);
565| 
566|         document.getElementById('popupAccept').onclick = () => {
567|             socket.emit('invitePrivate', { toPseudo: pseudo, fromPseudo: user.pseudo });
568|             popup.remove();
569|         };
570| 
571|         document.getElementById('popupDecline').onclick = () => {
572|             popup.remove();

579|         const chatPanel = document.querySelector('.chat-panel');
580|         if (!chatPanel) return;
581|

584|         }

587|         if (!inputArea) return;

615|             transition: opacity 0.2s ease, transform 0.2s ease;
616|         `;

619|             <span>🔔 <strong>${data.from}</strong> vous invite en chat privé.</span>
620|             <div style="display: flex; gap: 6px;">
621|                 <button id="inviteAccept" style="background:#27ae60; color:white; border:none; border-radius:4px; padding:4px 10px; cursor:pointer;">✅ Accepter</button>
622|                 <button id="inviteDecline" style="background:#e74c3c; color:white; border:none; border-radius:4px; padding:4px 10px; cursor:pointer;">❌ Refuser</button>
623|             </div>
624|         `;

627|

631|         }, 10);
632|

635|             popup.remove();
636|             alert(`💬 Chat privé ouvert avec ${data.from} !`);
637|         };
638| 
639|         document.getElementById('inviteDecline').onclick = () => {
640|             socket.emit('declinePrivateInvite', { fromPseudo: user.pseudo, toPseudo: data.from });
641|             popup.remove();
642|         };
643|     });
644| 
645|     // ========== POPUP SYSTÈME POUR RETOUR ARRIÈRE ==========
646|     let userHasInteracted = false;
647| 
648|     // Détecter toute interaction de l'utilisateur
649|     document.body.addEventListener('click', () => userHasInteracted = true, { once: true });
650|     document.body.addEventListener('keydown', () => userHasInteracted = true, { once: true });
651| 
652|     // Piège pour l'historique
653|     history.pushState(null, null, location.href);
654| 
655|     window.addEventListener('popstate', function (event) {
656|         if (!userHasInteracted) {
657|             // Pas d'interaction : on ne peut pas afficher de popup
658|             history.pushState(null, null, location.href);
659|             return;
660|         }
661| 
662|         // On ajoute beforeunload temporairement
663|         const beforeUnloadHandler = (e) => {
664|             e.preventDefault();
665|             e.returnValue = true;
666|         };
667| 
668|         window.addEventListener('beforeunload', beforeUnloadHandler);
669| 
670|         // Petit délai pour que beforeunload se déclenche
671|         setTimeout(() => {
672|             window.removeEventListener('beforeunload', beforeUnloadHandler);
673|         }, 500);
674| 
675|         history.pushState(null, null, location.href);
676|     });
677| 
678|     // Suppression en base avec sendBeacon (fiable)
679|     window.addEventListener('pagehide', () => {
680|         navigator.sendBeacon('/api/delete-user', JSON.stringify({ pseudo: user.pseudo }));
681|     });
682| 
683| 
684| }

# FILE: /var/www/meetgay/public/js/utils.js

1| // ========== FICHIER utils.js ==========
2| 
3| function escapeHtml(str) {
4|     if (!str) return '';
5|     return str.replace(/[&<>]/g, function (m) {
6|         if (m === '&') return '&amp;';
7|         if (m === '<') return '&lt;';
8|         if (m === '>') return '&gt;';
9|         return m;
10|     });
11| }
12| 
13| function formatTime(date) {
14|     return date.toLocaleTimeString([], { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' });
15| }
16| 
17| function getOrientationSymbol(tendencies) {
18|     if (tendencies === 'A') return '▲';
19|     if (tendencies === 'P') return '▼';
20|     return '▲▼';
21| }

24|     if (tendencies === 'A') return '▲ Actif';
25|     if (tendencies === 'P') return '▼ Passif';
26|     return '▲▼ Versatile';

233|             const pseudo = clean(document.getElementById('pseudo').value);
234|             const lowerPseudo = pseudo.toLowerCase();

236|

238|                 alert(currentLang === 'fr' ? "Ce pseudo contient un mot interdit" : "Deze gebruikersnaam bevat een verboden woord");
239|                 return;

245|             const gender = document.getElementById('gender').value;
246|             const purpose = document.getElementById('purpose').value;
247|             const location = document.getElementById('location').value;
248| 
249|             let missing = [];
250|             if (!age) missing.push('age');
251|             if (!tendencies) missing.push('tendencies');
252|             if (!gender) missing.push('gender');
253|             if (!purpose) missing.push('purpose');
254|             if (!location) missing.push('location');
255| 
256|             if (missing.length > 0) {
257|                 missing.forEach(field => highlightField(field));
258|                 alert(currentLang === 'fr' ? "Veuillez remplir tous les champs (champs en rouge)" : "Vul alle velden in (rode velden)");
259|                 return;
260|             }
261|             if (pseudo.length < 2 || pseudo.length > 15) {
262|                 alert(currentLang === 'fr' ? "Le pseudo doit faire entre 2 et 15 caractères" : "De gebruikersnaam moet 2-15 tekens bevatten");
263|                 return;
264|             }
265| 
266|             const user = {
267|                 pseudo, age: parseInt(age), tendencies, gender, purpose,
268|                 locationCode: location,
269|                 locationName: document.getElementById('location').selectedOptions[0]?.text || location, origine: origine || 'Non renseigné',
270|                 bio: bio.substring(0, 100) || (currentLang === 'fr' ? "Aucune présentation" : "Geen introductie"),
271|                 fingerprint: sessionStorage.getItem('fingerprint')
272|             };

274|             const submitBtn = document.getElementById('submitBtn');

282|                     headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
283|                     body: JSON.stringify(user)
284|                 });
285|                 const registerData = await registerRes.json();

287|                     if (registerData.error === 'Pseudo déjà utilisé') {
288|                         alert(currentLang === 'fr' ? "Ce pseudo est déjà utilisé" : "Deze gebruikersnaam is al in gebruik");
289|                     } else {
290|                         throw new Error(registerData.error || 'Erreur inscription');
291|                     }
292|                     submitBtn.disabled = false;
293|                     submitBtn.innerHTML = originalText;
294|                     return;
295|                 }
296|                 const loginRes = await fetch('/api/login', {

298|                     headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
299|                     body: JSON.stringify({ pseudo })
300|                 });

# FILE: /var/www/meetgay/public/js/fingerprint-source.js

1| ﻿import FingerprintJS from '@fingerprintjs/fingerprintjs';
2| 
3| (async () => {
4|     try {
5|         const fp = await FingerprintJS.load();
6|         const result = await fp.get();
7|         const visitorId = result.visitorId;
8|         sessionStorage.setItem('fingerprint', visitorId);
9|         window.currentFingerprint = visitorId;
10|         console.log('🔒 Fingerprint généré:', visitorId);
11|     } catch (err) {
12|         console.error('❌ Erreur fingerprint:', err);
13|         // Fallback temporaire (évite de bloquer l'utilisateur)
14|         const fallback = 'temp_' + Date.now();
15|         sessionStorage.setItem('fingerprint', fallback);
16|         window.currentFingerprint = fallback;
17|     }
18| })();

# FILE: /var/www/meetgay/public/js/common.js

1| ﻿// ========== COMMON - MeetGay ==========
2| // Fonctions et détecteurs partagés entre les pages (login, chat, etc.)
3| 
4| (function () {
5|     // ========== 1. Détection de la résolution d'écran ==========
6|     function detectResolution() {
7|         const width = window.innerWidth;
8|         const height = window.innerHeight;
9|         const resolution = `${width}x${height}`;
10|         sessionStorage.setItem('screen_resolution', resolution);
11|         console.log(`📱 Résolution détectée : ${resolution}`);
12|         return resolution;
13|     }
14| 
15|     // ========== 2. Échapper le HTML (sécurité) ==========
16|     function escapeHtml(str) {
17|         if (!str) return '';
18|         return str.replace(/[&<>]/g, (m) => {
19|             if (m === '&') return '&amp;';
20|             if (m === '<') return '&lt;';
21|             if (m === '>') return '&gt;';
22|             return m;
23|         });
24|     }
25| 
26|     // ========== 3. Formater l'heure (HH:MM) ==========
27|     function formatTime(date) {
28|         if (!date) return '';
29|         const d = new Date(date);
30|         return `${d.getHours().toString().padStart(2, '0')}:${d.getMinutes().toString().padStart(2, '0')}`;
31|     }
32| 
33|     // ========== 4. Exécuter la détection au chargement ==========
34|     if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
35|         document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', detectResolution);
36|     } else {
37|         detectResolution();
38|     }
39| 
40|     // ========== 5. Exposer les fonctions globalement ==========
41|     window.common = {
42|         escapeHtml: escapeHtml,
43|         formatTime: formatTime,
44|         detectResolution: detectResolution,
45|         getResolution: () => sessionStorage.getItem('screen_resolution')
46|     };
47| })();

# FILE: /var/www/meetgay/public/js/modal-handler-admin.js

1| ﻿// popup.js - Système de popup personnalisé
2| // Aucune dépendance, fonctionne sur tous les navigateurs
3| 
4| (function () {
5|     // Créer la structure HTML du popup (injectée automatiquement)
6|     function createPopupStructure() {
7|         if (document.getElementById('mg-popup-container')) return;

25|     // Configurer les boutons une fois que le DOM est prêt
26|     function setupButtons(onConfirm, onCancel) {
27|         const confirmBtn = document.getElementById('mg-popup-confirm');
28|         const cancelBtn = document.getElementById('mg-popup-cancel');
29|         const container = document.getElementById('mg-popup-container');
30| 
31|         if (confirmBtn) {
32|             const newConfirm = confirmBtn.cloneNode(true);
33|             confirmBtn.parentNode.replaceChild(newConfirm, confirmBtn);
34|             newConfirm.onclick = () => {
35|                 container.style.display = 'none';
36|                 if (onConfirm) onConfirm();
37|             };
38|         }
39| 
40|         if (cancelBtn) {
41|             const newCancel = cancelBtn.cloneNode(true);
42|             cancelBtn.parentNode.replaceChild(newCancel, cancelBtn);
43|             newCancel.onclick = () => {
44|                 container.style.display = 'none';
45|                 if (onCancel) onCancel();
46|             };
47|         }
48| 
49|         // Clic sur le fond noir pour fermer (optionnel)
50|         container.onclick = (e) => {
51|             if (e.target === container) {
52|                 container.style.display = 'none';
53|                 if (onCancel) onCancel();
54|             }
55|         };
56|     }

72|             setupButtons(options.onConfirm, options.onCancel);
73|

75|             container.style.display = 'flex';
76|         },
77|

79|             const container = document.getElementById('mg-popup-container');

81|         }

2| // Centralise toute la logique restante du chat (fingerprint, traductions, historique coulissant, menus)

4| (function () {
5|     // ========== 1. Fingerprint (si non déjà fait par fp-bundle.js) ==========
6|     (async function () {
7|         let fingerprint = sessionStorage.getItem('fingerprint');
8|         if (!fingerprint) {
9|             try {
10|                 // Si FingerprintJS est déjà chargé globalement, on l'utilise
11|                 if (typeof FingerprintJS !== 'undefined') {
12|                     const fp = await FingerprintJS.load();
13|                     const result = await fp.get();
14|                     fingerprint = result.visitorId;
15|                 } else {
16|                     console.warn('FingerprintJS non trouvé, utilisation d\'un identifiant aléatoire');
17|                     fingerprint = 'fp_' + Math.random().toString(36).substring(2);
18|                 }
19|                 sessionStorage.setItem('fingerprint', fingerprint);
20|                 window.currentFingerprint = fingerprint;
21|             } catch (err) {
22|                 console.error('❌ Fingerprint impossible à générer:', err);
23|                 fingerprint = 'fallback_' + Math.random().toString(36).substring(2);
24|                 sessionStorage.setItem('fingerprint', fingerprint);
25|                 window.currentFingerprint = fingerprint;
26|             }
27|         } else {
28|             window.currentFingerprint = fingerprint;
29|         }
30|     })();
31| 
32|     // ========== 2. Vérifier si l'utilisateur est en session ==========

37|             return;
38|         }

90|         let tabOffset = false;
91| 
92|         // Fonction pour décaler ou remettre le bouton
93|         function toggleTabOffset() {
94|             if (!historyTab) return;
95|             if (tabOffset) {
96|                 historyTab.style.right = '0';
97|                 tabOffset = false;
98|             } else {
99|                 historyTab.style.right = '-10px';
100|                 tabOffset = true;
101|             }
102|         }
103| 
104|         if (historyInner) {
105|             historyInner.classList.remove('open');
106|         }
107| 
108|         if (historyTab && historyInner) {
109|             historyTab.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
110|                 e.stopPropagation();
111|                 historyInner.classList.toggle('open');
112|                 toggleTabOffset(); // ← décaler/remettre le bouton au clic
113|             });
114|         }
115| 
116|         if (closeBtn && historyInner) {
117|             closeBtn.addEventListener('click', function () {
118|                 historyInner.classList.remove('open');
119|                 // Quand on ferme avec la croix, on remet aussi le bouton
120|                 if (historyTab) historyTab.style.right = '0';
121|                 tabOffset = false;
122|             });
123|         }
124|     });

126|     // ========== 6. Génération des menus (fenêtre droite) ==========
127|     // Note : ce bloc utilise import, il doit être dans un script type="module"
128|     // On va donc le charger dynamiquement
129|     // ========== 6. Génération des menus (fenêtre droite) ==========
130|     (function initMenus() {
131|         const menuList = document.getElementById('newMenusList');
132|         const windowContent = document.getElementById('windowContent');
133|         const windowPlaceholder = document.getElementById('windowPlaceholder');
134|

142|         fetch('/js/menus-data.js')

144|             .then(data => {
145|                 // Extraire les variables exportées (approche simple)
146|                 const exports = {};
147|                 const moduleCode = data.replace(/export const /g, 'exports.');
148|                 new Function('exports', moduleCode)(exports);
149|

162|                         windowContent.innerHTML = contents[menu.id] || '<div class="dynamic-content"><h3>Contenu à venir</h3></div>';
163|                     };
164|                     menuList.appendChild(item);
165|                 });
166|             })
167|             .catch(err => console.error('Erreur chargement menus-data.js:', err));

187|     // mobile-nav.js - Navigation mobile adaptative
188|     (function () {
189|         'use strict';
190| 
191|         // Lecture des media queries CSS (vous les modifiez dans le CSS)
192|         const desktopMQ = window.matchMedia('(min-width: 1081px)');
193|         const mobileMQ = window.matchMedia('(max-width: 350px)');
194|         // Entre 351px et 1080px = mode desktop également
195| 
196|         // === VERSION DESKTOP ===
197|         function initDesktopVersion() {
198|             const nav = document.getElementById('mobileNav');
199|             const panel = document.getElementById('navSettingsPanel');
200|             const settingsBtn = document.getElementById('navSettingsBtn');
201|             const navButtons = document.querySelectorAll('.mobile-nav button:not(#toggleNavBtn)');
202| 
203|             let isPanelOpen = false;
204|             let animationTimer = null;
205| 
206|             if (nav) nav.style.display = 'flex';
207| 
208|             // Bouton bleu
209|             const oldToggleBtn = document.getElementById('toggleNavBtn');
210|             if (oldToggleBtn) {
211|                 const newToggleBtn = oldToggleBtn.cloneNode(true);
212|                 oldToggleBtn.parentNode.replaceChild(newToggleBtn, oldToggleBtn);
213|                 newToggleBtn.onclick = function (e) {
214|                     e.preventDefault();
215|                     const isVisible = navButtons[0]?.classList.contains('hidden');
216|                     navButtons.forEach(btn => {
217|                         if (isVisible) btn.classList.remove('hidden');
218|                         else btn.classList.add('hidden');
219|                     });
220|                     localStorage.setItem('mobileNavVisible', !isVisible);
221|                 };
222|             }
223| 
224|             function setPanelOrientation() {
225|                 if (!panel || !nav) return;
226|                 const pos = nav.getAttribute('data-position') || 'bottom';
227|                 panel.classList.remove('horizontal', 'vertical');
228|                 if (pos === 'left' || pos === 'right') {
229|                     panel.classList.add('vertical');
230|                 } else {
231|                     panel.classList.add('horizontal');
232|                 }
233|             }
234| 
235|             function positionPanel() {
236|                 if (!panel || !nav) return;
237|                 const navRect = nav.getBoundingClientRect();
238|                 const panelW = panel.offsetWidth;
239|                 const panelH = panel.offsetHeight;
240|                 const pos = nav.getAttribute('data-position') || 'bottom';
241|                 if (panelW === 0 || panelH === 0) return;
242| 
243|                 let top, left;
244|                 switch (pos) {
245|                     case 'left':
246|                         left = navRect.right + 8;
247|                         top = navRect.top + (navRect.height / 2) - (panelH / 2);
248|                         break;
249|                     case 'right':
250|                         left = navRect.left - panelW - 8;
251|                         top = navRect.top + (navRect.height / 2) - (panelH / 2);
252|                         break;
253|                     case 'top':
254|                         left = navRect.left;
255|                         top = navRect.bottom + 8;
256|                         break;
257|                     default:
258|                         left = navRect.left;
259|                         top = navRect.top - panelH - 8;
260|                         break;
261|                 }
262| 
263|                 if (left < 5) left = 5;
264|                 if (left + panelW > window.innerWidth - 5) left = window.innerWidth - panelW - 5;
265|                 if (top < 5) top = 5;
266|                 if (top + panelH > window.innerHeight - 5) {
267|                     if (pos === 'top') top = navRect.top - panelH - 8;
268|                     else if (pos === 'bottom') top = navRect.bottom + 8;
269|                     else top = window.innerHeight - panelH - 5;
270|                 }
271| 
272|                 panel.style.top = top + 'px';
273|                 panel.style.left = left + 'px';
274|             }
275| 
276|             function openPanel() {
277|                 if (!panel) return;
278|                 panel.style.display = 'flex';
279|                 isPanelOpen = true;
280|                 setPanelOrientation();
281|                 positionPanel();
282|             }
283| 
284|             function closePanel() {
285|                 if (!panel) return;
286|                 panel.style.display = 'none';
287|                 isPanelOpen = false;
288|                 if (animationTimer) clearTimeout(animationTimer);
289|             }
290| 
291|             function togglePanel(e) {
292|                 e.stopPropagation();
293|                 if (isPanelOpen) closePanel();
294|                 else openPanel();
295|             }
296| 
297|             function setNavPosition(position) {
298|                 if (!nav) return;
299|                 nav.setAttribute('data-position', position);
300|                 localStorage.setItem('mobileNavPosition', position);
301|                 if (isPanelOpen) {
302|                     if (animationTimer) clearTimeout(animationTimer);
303|                     animationTimer = setTimeout(() => {
304|                         setPanelOrientation();
305|                         positionPanel();
306|                         animationTimer = null;
307|                     }, 320);
308|                 }
309|             }
310| 
311|             function loadSavedSettings() {
312|                 const savedPos = localStorage.getItem('mobileNavPosition');
313|                 if (savedPos && ['top', 'bottom', 'left', 'right'].includes(savedPos)) {
314|                     nav.setAttribute('data-position', savedPos);
315|                 } else {
316|                     nav.setAttribute('data-position', 'bottom');
317|                 }
318|                 const savedVis = localStorage.getItem('mobileNavVisible');
319|                 if (savedVis === 'true') navButtons.forEach(btn => btn.classList.add('hidden'));
320|                 else if (savedVis === 'false') navButtons.forEach(btn => btn.classList.remove('hidden'));
321|             }
322| 
323|             function resetAll() {
324|                 closePanel();
325|                 localStorage.removeItem('mobileNavPosition');
326|                 localStorage.removeItem('mobileNavVisible');
327|                 location.reload();
328|             }
329| 
330|             function handleClickOutside(e) {
331|                 if (!isPanelOpen) return;
332|                 if (!nav.contains(e.target) && !panel.contains(e.target)) closePanel();
333|             }
334| 
335|             function scrollToTarget(e) {
336|                 const btn = e.currentTarget;
337|                 const targetId = btn.getAttribute('data-target');
338|                 if (!targetId) return;
339|                 e.preventDefault();
340|                 const target = document.getElementById(targetId);
341|                 if (target) {
342|                     closePanel();
343|                     const offset = nav.getAttribute('data-position') === 'top' ? nav.offsetHeight + 20 : 80;
344|                     const pos = target.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.scrollY - offset;
345|                     window.scrollTo({ top: pos, behavior: 'smooth' });
346|                 }
347|             }
348| 
349|             if (nav && panel) {
350|                 loadSavedSettings();
351|                 if (settingsBtn) settingsBtn.onclick = togglePanel;
352|                 document.getElementById('navPosTop')?.addEventListener('click', () => setNavPosition('top'));
353|                 document.getElementById('navPosBottom')?.addEventListener('click', () => setNavPosition('bottom'));
354|                 document.getElementById('navPosLeft')?.addEventListener('click', () => setNavPosition('left'));
355|                 document.getElementById('navPosRight')?.addEventListener('click', () => setNavPosition('right'));
356|                 document.getElementById('navReset')?.addEventListener('click', resetAll);
357|                 document.querySelectorAll('[data-target]').forEach(btn => {
358|                     btn.addEventListener('click', scrollToTarget);
359|                 });
360|                 document.addEventListener('click', handleClickOutside);
361|                 window.addEventListener('resize', () => { if (isPanelOpen) positionPanel(); });
362|             }
363|         }
364| 
365|         // === VERSION MOBILE (très petits écrans) ===
366|         function initMobileVersion() {
367|             const oldNav = document.getElementById('mobileNav');
368|             if (oldNav) oldNav.style.display = 'none';
369| 
370|             let menuBtn = document.getElementById('mobileMenuBtn');
371|             if (!menuBtn) {
372|                 menuBtn = document.createElement('button');
373|                 menuBtn.id = 'mobileMenuBtn';
374|                 menuBtn.innerHTML = '☰';
375|                 document.body.appendChild(menuBtn);
376|             }
377|

379|             if (!panel) {
380|                 panel = document.createElement('div');
381|                 panel.id = 'mobileNavPanel';
382|                 panel.innerHTML = `
383|                 <div class="mobile-panel-buttons">
384|                     <button data-target="connectes">👥<span>Connectés</span></button>
385|                     <button data-target="chat">💬<span>Chat</span></button>
386|                     <button data-target="new-window">📦<span>Nouveau</span></button>
387|                     <button data-target="menus">📋<span>Menus</span></button>
388|                 </div>
389|             `;
390|                 document.body.appendChild(panel);
391|             }
392| 
393|             let isOpen = false;
394| 
395|             function openPanel() {
396|                 panel.classList.add('open');
397|                 isOpen = true;
398|             }
399| 
400|             function closePanel() {
401|                 panel.classList.remove('open');
402|                 isOpen = false;
403|             }
404| 
405|             function togglePanel() {
406|                 if (isOpen) closePanel();
407|                 else openPanel();
408|             }
409| 
410|             function scrollToTarget(e) {
411|                 const btn = e.currentTarget;
412|                 const targetId = btn.getAttribute('data-target');

425|             });
426| 
427|             document.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
428|                 if (isOpen && !panel.contains(e.target) && e.target !== menuBtn) {
429|                     closePanel();
430|                 }
431|             });
432|         }
433| 
434|         // === LANCEMENT (basé sur les media queries CSS) ===
435|         function detectAndInit() {
436|             if (mobileMQ.matches) {
437|                 initMobileVersion();
438|             } else {
439|                 initDesktopVersion();
440|             }
441|         }
442| 
443|         detectAndInit();
444| 
445|         // === REDIMENSIONNEMENT ===
446|         let resizeTimer;
447|         desktopMQ.addEventListener('change', function () {
448|             if (resizeTimer) clearTimeout(resizeTimer);
449|             resizeTimer = setTimeout(() => location.reload(), 150);
450|         });
451|         mobileMQ.addEventListener('change', function () {
452|             if (resizeTimer) clearTimeout(resizeTimer);
453|             resizeTimer = setTimeout(() => location.reload(), 150);
454|         });

1| <!DOCTYPE html>
2| <html lang="fr">
3| 
4| <head>
5|     <meta charset="UTF-8">
6|     <title>Login Admin - MeetGay</title>
7|     <!-- CSS communs -->
8|     <link rel="stylesheet" href="/css/common/reset.css">
9| 
10|     <!-- CSS spécifique admin-login -->
11|     <link rel="stylesheet" href="/css/pages/admin-login.css">
12| </head>
13| 
14| <body>
15|     <div class="login-box">
16|         <h1>👑 Admin Login</h1>
17|         <input type="text" id="adminUsername" placeholder="Nom d'utilisateur">
18|         <input type="password" id="adminPassword" placeholder="Mot de passe">
19|         <button onclick="loginAdmin()">Se connecter</button>
20|         <div id="errorMsg" class="error"></div>
21|     </div>
22| 
23|     <script>
24|         async function loginAdmin() {
25|             const username = document.getElementById('adminUsername').value;
26|             const password = document.getElementById('adminPassword').value;
27|             const errorDiv = document.getElementById('errorMsg');
28| 
29|             if (!username || !password) {
30|                 errorDiv.textContent = 'Veuillez entrer nom d\'utilisateur et mot de passe';
31|                 return;
32|             }
33| 
34|             try {
35|                 const response = await fetch('/api/admin/login', {
36|                     method: 'POST',
37|                     headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
38|                     body: JSON.stringify({ username, password })
39|                 });
40| 
41|                 const data = await response.json();
42| 
43|                 if (data.success) {
44|                     // ⚠️ PLUS DE TOKEN, REDIRECTION SIMPLE
45|                     window.location.href = '/admin.html';
46|                 } else {
47|                     errorDiv.textContent = data.error || 'Identifiants incorrects';
48|                 }
49|             } catch (err) {
50|                 errorDiv.textContent = 'Erreur de connexion';
51|             }
52|         }
53|     </script>
54| </body>
55| 
56| </html>

73|     <script>
74|         const ageSelect = document.getElementById('ageSelect');
75|         const btnFr = document.getElementById('btnFr');
76|         const btnNl = document.getElementById('btnNl');
77|         const ageError = document.getElementById('ageError');
78| 
79|         btnFr.disabled = true;
80|         btnNl.disabled = true;
81| 
82|         ageSelect.addEventListener('change', function () {
83|             const selectedValue = ageSelect.value;
84| 
85|             if (selectedValue === '18plus') {
86|                 btnFr.disabled = false;
87|                 btnNl.disabled = false;
88|                 ageError.classList.remove('show');
89|             }
90|             else if (selectedValue === '18moins') {
91|                 btnFr.disabled = true;
92|                 btnNl.disabled = true;
93|                 ageError.classList.add('show');
94|             }
95|             else {
96|                 btnFr.disabled = true;
97|                 btnNl.disabled = true;
98|                 ageError.classList.remove('show');
99|             }
100|         });
101| 
102|         function setAgeVerified() {
103|             sessionStorage.setItem('meetgay_age_verified', 'true');
104|             sessionStorage.setItem('meetgay_age_verified_time', Date.now());
105|         }
106| 
107|         function chooseLanguage(lang) {
108|             if (ageSelect.value !== '18plus') {
109|                 ageError.classList.add('show');
110|                 return;
111|             }
112|             setAgeVerified();
113|             localStorage.setItem('MeetGay_lang', lang);
114|             window.location.href = '/login.html';
115|         }
116| 
117|         btnFr.onclick = () => chooseLanguage('fr');
118|         btnNl.onclick = () => chooseLanguage('nl');
119|     </script>
120| </body>
121| 
122| </html>

651|                 { pseudo: "Alex", age: 24, ville: "Bruxelles", purpose: "Discussion", bio: "Fan de voyages" },

658|             function renderUsers() {
659|                 const container = document.getElementById('usersList');
660|                 if (!container) return;
661|                 if (onlineUsers.length === 0) {
662|                     container.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-message">Aucun connecté</div>';
663|                     return;
664|                 }
665|                 container.innerHTML = '';
666|                 onlineUsers.forEach(user => {
667|                     const div = document.createElement('div');
668|                     div.className = 'user-item';
669|                     if (currentTarget && currentTarget.pseudo === user.pseudo) div.classList.add('current-target');
670|                     div.innerHTML = `<strong>${user.pseudo}</strong> (${user.age} ans, ${user.ville})<br><small>${user.purpose || "En ligne"}</small>`;
671|                     div.onclick = () => selectUser(user);
672|                     container.appendChild(div);
673|                 });
674|                 document.getElementById('onlineCount').innerText = onlineUsers.length;
675|             }
676| 
677|             function selectUser(user) {
678|                 currentTarget = user;
679|                 renderUsers();
680| 
681|                 document.getElementById('contactName').innerText = user.pseudo;
682|                 document.getElementById('contactAge').innerText = user.age;
683|                 document.getElementById('contactPurpose').innerHTML = `<i class="fas fa-tag"></i> ${user.purpose || "Discussion"}`;
684|                 document.getElementById('contactBio').innerHTML = user.bio ? `<i class="fas fa-quote-left"></i> ${user.bio}` : '';
685|                 document.getElementById('contactInfo').style.display = 'block';
686|

688|                 const sendBtn = document.getElementById('sendBtn');
689|                 input.disabled = false;

691|                 input.placeholder = `Message pour ${user.pseudo}...`;
692|

694|                 renderMessages(user.pseudo);
695|             }
696| 
697|             function renderMessages(pseudo) {
698|                 const msgArea = document.getElementById('messageArea');
699|                 const userMessages = messages[pseudo] || [];
700|                 if (userMessages.length === 0) {
701|                     msgArea.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-message"><i class="fas fa-comment"></i> En attente de message...</div>';
702|                     return;
703|                 }
704|                 msgArea.innerHTML = '';
705|                 userMessages.forEach(msg => {
706|                     const bubble = document.createElement('div');
707|                     bubble.className = `message-bubble ${msg.from === currentUser.pseudo ? 'message-mine' : 'message-theirs'}`;
708|                     bubble.innerHTML = `<div>${msg.text}</div><div class="message-time">${msg.time}</div>`;
709|                     msgArea.appendChild(bubble);
710|                 });
711|                 msgArea.scrollTop = msgArea.scrollHeight;
712|             }
713| 
714|             function sendMessage() {
715|                 if (!currentTarget) return;
716|                 const input = document.getElementById('messageInput');
717|                 const text = input.value.trim();
718|                 if (!text) return;
719|                 const msg = {
720|                     from: currentUser.pseudo,
721|                     text: text,
722|                     time: new Date().toLocaleTimeString([], { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' })
723|                 };
724|                 if (!messages[currentTarget.pseudo]) messages[currentTarget.pseudo] = [];
725|                 messages[currentTarget.pseudo].push(msg);
726|                 renderMessages(currentTarget.pseudo);
727|                 input.value = '';
728|             }
729|

731|                 { id: 'profil', icon: 'fa-user-circle', title: 'Mon Profil' },

110|     <script>
111|         const contactForm = document.getElementById('contactForm');
112|         const statusDiv = document.getElementById('statusMessage');
113| 
114|         // Remplir la résolution détectée
115|         const resolutionField = document.getElementById('resolution');
116|         const savedResolution = sessionStorage.getItem('screen_resolution');
117|         if (savedResolution) {
118|             resolutionField.value = savedResolution;
119|         } else {
120|             resolutionField.value = window.innerWidth + 'x' + window.innerHeight;
121|         }
122| 
123|         // ========== Gestion affichage des champs techniques ==========
124|         const subjectSelect = document.getElementById('subject');
125|         const resolutionGroup = document.getElementById('resolutionGroup');
126|         const userEnvGroup = document.getElementById('userEnvGroup');
127| 
128|         function toggleTechFields() {
129|             if (subjectSelect.value === 'bug') {
130|                 resolutionGroup.style.display = 'block';
131|                 userEnvGroup.style.display = 'block';
132|             } else {
133|                 resolutionGroup.style.display = 'none';
134|                 userEnvGroup.style.display = 'none';
135|             }
136|         }
137| 
138|         subjectSelect.addEventListener('change', toggleTechFields);
139|         toggleTechFields(); // Initialisation au chargement
140| 
141|         // ========== Envoi du formulaire ==========
142|         contactForm.addEventListener('submit', async (e) => {
143|             e.preventDefault();
144| 
145|             const formData = {
146|                 name: document.getElementById('name').value.trim(),
147|                 email: document.getElementById('email').value.trim(),
148|                 subject: subjectSelect.value,
149|                 message: document.getElementById('message').value.trim(),
150|                 resolution: resolutionField.value,
151|                 userEnv: document.getElementById('userEnv').value.trim()
152|             };
153| 
154|             // Si le sujet est "bug", on ajoute les infos techniques dans le message
155|             if (formData.subject === 'bug') {
156|                 const resolution = sessionStorage.getItem('screen_resolution') || `${window.innerWidth}x${window.innerHeight}`;
157|                 const userAgent = navigator.userAgent;
158|                 formData.message += `\n\n--- Informations techniques (automatique) ---\nRésolution : ${resolution}\nNavigateur : ${userAgent}`;
159|             }
160| 
161|             // Validation
162|             if (!formData.name || !formData.email || !formData.subject || !formData.message) {
163|                 showStatus('❌ Veuillez remplir tous les champs obligatoires', 'error');
164|                 return;
165|             }
166| 
167|             if (!formData.email.includes('@')) {
168|                 showStatus('❌ Email invalide', 'error');
169|                 return;
170|             }
171| 
172|             const submitBtn = document.querySelector('.submit-btn');
173|             submitBtn.disabled = true;
174|             submitBtn.textContent = '⏳ Envoi en cours...';
175| 
176|             try {
177|                 const response = await fetch('/api/contact', {
178|                     method: 'POST',
179|                     headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
180|                     body: JSON.stringify(formData)
181|                 });
182| 
183|                 const data = await response.json();
184| 
185|                 if (response.ok && data.success) {
186|                     showStatus('✅ Message envoyé ! Nous vous répondrons rapidement.', 'success');
187|                     contactForm.reset();
188|                     // Remettre les champs techniques en état après reset
189|                     toggleTechFields();
190|                 } else {
191|                     showStatus('❌ Erreur : ' + (data.error || 'Réessayez plus tard'), 'error');
192|                 }
193|             } catch (err) {
194|                 console.error('Erreur envoi:', err);
195|                 showStatus('❌ Erreur réseau. Vérifiez votre connexion.', 'error');
196|             } finally {
197|                 submitBtn.disabled = false;
198|                 submitBtn.textContent = '📨 Envoyer le message';
199|             }
200|         });
201| 
202|         function showStatus(message, type) {
203|             statusDiv.textContent = message;
204|             statusDiv.className = `status-message ${type}`;
205|             statusDiv.style.display = 'block';
206| 
207|             setTimeout(() => {
208|                 statusDiv.style.display = 'none';
209|             }, 5000);
210|         }
211|     </script>
212| </body>
213| 
214| </html>
